1Ô∏è‚É£ Accommodation and services
  Of course, there is nothing to say about the quality of the accommodation and other services. Someone from the hotel will call to confirm at around 7 o'clock the night before check-in. A steward will then be assigned, and all steward questions will be answered promptly in the group. The butler had already been waiting at the visitor center before arriving, and trotted along to lead the vehicle to the VIP parking lot to arrange parking. Due to the Spring Festival period. If there are too many tourists, we will not arrange to check in by boat, but will arrive by tour bus instead.
  The health condition is very good. I don‚Äôt know how much cleaner it is compared to the previous Naked Shopping Center with the same price. The hygiene level in the room is one of the few in the hotel. In particular, I found that the hotel's bath towels have corresponding QR codes. After scanning, I found that it is a visual tracking of the cleaning status.
   Needless to say the service is good. Everywhere you go in the hotel, there are service staff who greet you with a sincere smile. Knowing that there are only 33 rooms in the entire hotel, it seems that the number of service staff must be equal to the number of guests in order to provide such meticulous service. Every time you enter or leave the hotel, the waiter will run in front of you to open the door for you, warm and polite.
  Final departure is arranged to board the boat at the hotel's private pier. We left the hotel in a rowing boat for half an hour, and then took a final tour of the entire Wuzhen waterway. The feeling of Oriental Venice was particularly strong.
2Ô∏è‚É£Food
Special comments are made about the hotel restaurant, in addition to the exquisite and delicious breakfast (not many varieties, but each piece is exquisite). The food served is also amazing. Although during the Spring Festival, there are mainly set meals and there are not many a la carte varieties, but the quality is amazing! How many expensive restaurants can't do this? Just look at the parts of this bacon, the proportions of each piece are so golden, and your mouth is full of oil and milky flavor after one bite. Don't worry about stepping on any thunder at all, they are all delicious.
Wuzhen's tourism management level is civilized in the industry, and the silk industry adds even more color to Wuzhen
In short, Wuzhen is worth recommending, and the silk industry is even more highly recommended.

msg:Two days before my departure, I received a call from the Wuzhen Tourist Service Center, informing me that the Yida Silk Industry I booked was under maintenance and I could not move in. They directly changed me to a king-bed room with a view in the Jintang Hotel. After I expressed my dissatisfaction, Reluctantly changed to a suite in Jintang Hotel. However, when I arrived, I found out that Yida Silk Industry was operating normally, so what kind of mysterious operation is this? ? On the day I made the reservation, I called the Wuzhen service center to confirm whether the reservation was successful... Since they are all forced to arrange hotels, it is better to explain it directly to the tourists, disappointed!
